msg:Objective evaluation! This time I stayed at Hyatt, InterContinental, and Marriott. The prices of these three hotels are similar, but the service and quality are very different! 
[1] First of all, let me talk about the service: Marriott's hotels are getting more and more outrageous, and the service quality has seriously declined. I think I don't get along with Marriott hotels. I have given bad reviews more than once, and I have encountered bizarre experiences every time. 
From the moment I got off the car, there was no concierge service, and I had to carry my luggage in by myself. The lobby was chaotic and no one led me to check in. I went to the front desk to check in by myself. Several staff members in the lobby were busy with their phones, and I found this situation several times during my stay. 
The front desk said that I would be upgraded to an executive room, and when I entered the room, there was a strong smell of cigarettes. A hotel with all indoor smoking is non-smoking. I don't understand why the same thing happens every time I stay in Marriott hotels. Don't they check the sanitation? Is the smoke alarm just for decoration? I immediately asked the customer service to change the room, but I ended up waiting in the room for more than 20 minutes. During this period, I called to urge once, but in the end, no one led me to change the room. I went downstairs to the front desk to handle it in anger, and finally the manager took me there and apologized. At this time, the service improved. 
[2] Facilities and configuration: It may be the construction quality of Xiangtou. It can be said to be very rough and cheap. The place where the elevator comes out is not connected to the ground smoothly. The sewer can be blocked even when taking a shower. I once felt that the procurement was not Marriott but Xiangtou. I had the illusion of saving costs everywhere. 
There were no makeup remover cotton pads, only two cotton pads, and the paper box was empty after two sheets were taken. . . 
There were also strange gradings. For example, the executive room I was given at the beginning was smaller than the ordinary room. As shown in Figures 2 and 3, the difference can be seen by looking at the position of the sofa and bed beside the bed. The reason is that you can see the lake view. I also put two pictures of the lake view of the guest room for comparison. Anyway, I don‚Äôt think there is much difference. The executive room with a small room area is equipped with a coffee machine, while the ordinary room with a large room area does not. 
In addition, it may be the worst gym equipment of the Marriott hotel brand that I have stayed in. The back stretching equipment is not even adjusted. One is high and the other is low. The floor is not flat and it feels a little empty underneath. . . 
The last few stars are for the concierge manager, which may be the only good service during the stay.

The room was very nice and new, with complete facilities and a great view. The crib was just enough for my 14-month-old baby, who was 82cm tall. I think babies taller than 90cm don't need to apply for a crib. You can refer to this part. I would like to thank the aunt in the housekeeping department on the 59th floor for her hard work

The buffet on the second floor has three breakfasts and two dinners. I got to know all the staff. I would also like to thank the managers and aunts who worked hard on duty during the May Day holiday on behalf of my child. From receiving guests to seating to arranging waiters, everything was in order. They were very kind to the child and provided a lot of convenience. I would also like to thank the roast duck uncle on behalf of my child. My child is older and is no longer interested in ready-made complementary foods. The hotel's buffet completely solves the dining needs and really saves my life! From the experience of adults, we have also eaten all the hotel buffets in Beijing. This buffet is absolutely OK in terms of price and ingredients. It is definitely very cost-effective for guests staying in the hotel. Recommended

The service staff in the lobby are kind and in place. Various friendly reminders have been released for the children's mischief. In addition, the food delivery robot is well received. Hahahaha, it's too smart! Learn more

We have been to the gym and swimming pool on the 6th floor. The facilities are very complete. Business travelers must like it very much!

The executive bar on the 61st floor is included in our room rate. We also took our children to experience it. The service is very good. There are also drinks and so on. It is also business travel-friendly!

In short, it is a very suitable hotel for business travel. It is also good for tourists because the location is very good. It is not far from East Lake, Wuhan University, Yellow Crane Tower, Yangtze River Bridge, Chuhe Han Street, etc. For parents and children, this hotel is not a hotel specifically positioned for parents and children. There are definitely no large-scale amusement facilities. On rainy days, children's entertainment is to keep walking on all floors of the hotel. Hahaha But because the staff is very nice, the children are treated very well. Thank you again
